Reflection on Myself and the History of Providence
 [Prayer] 
 Today is October 26, 1980. Looking back on this day last year, it is a day of remembrance marking the first anniversary of President Park's passing. May the deceased be protected by the Father in the spirit world, and may this day be a day of remembrance that allows me to love the Republic of Korea even more. 
 Among the hearts of 30 million people, may the deep love of heaven come upon all those who cannot forget this day. I sincerely hope that all the sorrowful stories of national lamentation will become the foundation for future history and allow us to experience heaven's compassion once again.
 During this new year, may the Father bless all the key figures of the current government, centered around the former president, who are laying the groundwork for a new nation on the foundation of the hard work the Father has done, so that they can solemnly follow the path that heaven desires, while reflecting on the legacy left behind by the deceased and resolving the historical mistakes. I pray once again for this blessing.
 The unification groups scattered around the world are longing for this place, yearning for the land of Korea, and with their hearts longing for where their parents are, I believe they have already resolved to pray toward the Republic of Korea for a year. I sincerely hope that the land of Korea, which they long for as a providential homeland, will be blessed, and that in the future, the Republic of Korea can become a leader in the world and a standard-bearer in establishing heaven's will, so that the Father can adjust the providential historical direction and connect it to a foundation that can be proudly celebrated in the end. 
 Father! Please remember your gathered children. As we commemorate this day, may your holy hand not depart from this gathering, and may you weave our hearts together, allowing your love to dwell in the hearts of the unification movement and simultaneously fulfilling the solemn and sacred mission of allowing God's love to dwell in the hearts of all people through the Unification Church. I earnestly ask that this day become a day of celebration that inspires a solemn and holy resolve and belief to become your chosen people.
 Have compassion on the children gathered here. I thank you before the Father who has allowed us a higher connection to life through your words, and I wish to stand before this glorious moment without shame as your child, worthy of receiving love. I ask that a higher blessing be with us at this time, and I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
 [Message] The content I will share today is 'Reflection on Myself and the History of Providence.' I will speak briefly on this topic. 
 The history of providence is a history aimed at fulfilling the purpose of creation.
 As humans live their lives, when they reach their later years and approach the end of life, they tend to reflect on their lives. They reflect on how they spent their youth, how they lived their middle age, and how they have spent their old age. In that moment of reflection, they will judge for themselves whether their life was 'meaningful,' 'sad,' 'good,' or 'bad.' Just as individuals do this, nations do the same, and we can think that God's position in advancing the history of providence is also similar.
 When we consider from God's perspective, God has a holy will to establish the purpose of creation and to continue all of creation's history in order to pass on that great work to humanity. It is certain that this history continued because God hoped for a time when humanity and God could align in heart and spirit.
 Furthermore, from humanity's perspective, in order to inherit God's great work of creation, the same position applies. It is believed that a day will come when God's will, God's heart, and God's spirit can align with humanity's heart, and that this alignment will determine the fulfillment of the purpose of creation along with the inheritance of God's great work.
 The same applies to an individual's life. If one sets a good purpose and dedicates all their efforts and life to fulfilling that purpose, then that place will undoubtedly be a position that resonates with that person's heart or a place where they can love that person's purpose. In order to pass that on to their children or anyone else, the heart's position must be the same, and then the position of love must also be the same. Only then can it be passed down in a natural manner. This is an undeniable fact.
 God's purpose of creation to achieve a world united with God and humanity
 In this light, today, I would like to reflect once more on God's position from the perspective of 'Reflection on the History of Providence and Myself.' When we consider creation, we cannot see it as simply spoken into existence as the established churches think today. Centered on all of God's intentions, if we speak of the principles of our Unification Church, it is based on principles that establish God's will, and centered on that will, the purpose of creation was fulfilled through that course.
 So what is that principle? It is that all subjects and objects must become completely one. Without that, the will cannot be established. In establishing all environmental conditions, there must be a subjective or objective environment that is established, and in the oneness of the subject and object, the common purpose will be realized. It is an undeniable fact that the matters of love and all related issues develop from the realization of that common purpose.
 In this view, God's creation is undoubtedly a creation made with utmost sincerity centered on the will. There is nothing from the smallest animal to all plants or minerals that is not made with utmost sincerity. It does not go through a hypothetical process but goes through principles and laws, and those principles and laws must have a subject-object relationship.
 Furthermore, we must think that there can be no will apart from the subject and object. Love without a subject and object, and feelings without a subject and object, are naturally impossible conclusions. In this view, when we look through all the intentions that God created, the fact that God hoped for the fulfillment of the ideal of creation centered on the purpose of creation indicates that if God is the subject, then it is certain that He desired the formation of a relative humanity.
 Therefore, humanity and God were to become one centered on the will. The position of unity centered on the will is also the same in heart, the same in spirit, and the same in direction and activity. If the subject goes east, the object must follow east; if the subject goes together, the object must also go together. If the subject stops while going, the object must also stop; if the subject rests, the object must also rest. We can conclude that it is essential to go through a shared destiny. In this view, God and humanity share a decisive relationship of destiny.
 Therefore, when we view it centered on God's will, God Himself must also go through such a position, and we humans must also go through such a position. Thus, we can affirm that we are in a position of shared destiny, shared direction, and shared circumstances.
13 
The Purpose of Creation Broken by Humanity's Fall
 In this view, did God and humanity truly see the point of unity in the will? Just as the Bible presents today, humanity has fallen. What does that fall mean? It means that the point of unity in the will was not seen. Not only the will but also, furthermore, the emotional unity was not seen. Therefore, the question of when the point of unity in the will and the point of emotional unity will be determined between this human world and heaven remains a historical issue. Thus, in order to achieve the unity of the will and the unity of the heart, all those who engage with providence must be mobilized. It is an undeniable fact that God, who carries out providence, has led the direction of history toward the point of unity in the will by mobilizing all those who engage with providence.
 From the day the Adam family fell, God worked through Abel. Because of the parents' mistake, He worked through the children. What is the purpose of that providence? The purpose of providence is to establish the will, and what is the purpose of the will? It is to fulfill the ideal of creation and the purpose of creation. What does the fulfillment of the purpose of creation entail? It is the unity of love and the realization of ideals. Therefore, the fact that this did not come to fruition in the Adam family is seen as the fall. Thus, we know well that the fall of the will and the fall of the heart were established.
 In order to restore this, to recreate this, Abel was established and worked. Then, should Abel's will be separated from God's will? No, it must be united. Then, is the dimension that God sees aligned with the position that Abel is facing? The dimensions may differ, but in terms of direction, in the position that Abel, as an individual, faces before God's overall will, there are certainly differences, but in the process of carrying out the will, the positions and directions of the will must be aligned. This is undeniable.
 Therefore, in order to fulfill the providence of salvation, Abel must become one with Cain. The issue is how to unify Cain.
 What happened to the direction of the will? Due to the fall, it could not follow the normal path and began to operate along an abnormal path. Therefore, from God's perspective, this was not joy but sorrow. Furthermore, standing in an unnatural position, it could not help but shift the direction of the will. This is seen as a tragedy and an infinite suffering.
 Fallen humanity must follow the path of restoration through indemnity.
 However, in going through Abel, it is not possible to say, 'Hey, Abel! Come directly before me.' It must be done through Cain. There is this issue. Why is that? The content of indemnity restoration spoken of in the Unification Church is unavoidable. The sins committed by humanity cannot simply be overlooked according to the principle of cause and effect. If evil is done, one must receive the consequences of evil. If good is done, there must be consequences of good. Because one is in a position to pay the equivalent price, the condition of indemnity is established.
 So what is the condition of indemnity? Is it to walk the path that humanity wishes to walk? No. It is to walk the path that one does not wish to walk. Those in the satanic world may cry and resist, but those who follow heaven's will cannot fulfill God's will while crying and resisting. The essence of the will does not lead one to cry and resist. One must go through difficulties with hope, even in the midst of hardships. No matter how much one suffers, one must stand in a position of hope, proclaiming victory for tomorrow, and align with the direction of God's will. One must bear hope and carry the future's aspirations, overcoming and digesting the environment. This is the path that follows the will after the fall, and you must understand this clearly.
15 
So why can one not go directly? This is the issue. Because one cannot go directly, numerous complex problems centered around various religions have accumulated through the historical process. They are layered upon each other.
 If one cannot complete the path of the will that an individual must walk, one cannot emerge on the path of the will that a family must walk. Furthermore, if a family cannot emerge on the path of the will that it can complete, one cannot find the path of completion for tribes, nations, the world, and the entire cosmos, including the spirit world.
 In light of this conclusion, when we view God's position in advancing the history of providence today, has there ever been such a time? There has never been such a time. Then why has it come to this? It is because of the fall of Adam and Eve.
 If Adam and Eve had not fallen, what would have happened? The point of unity in the will would have begun from that day. In other words, with the start of the will, one would have naturally begun on a normal trajectory to fulfill the purpose of creation. Therefore, as long as one aligns with that period, one would naturally move toward the stage of fulfilling the purpose of creation. It is not a matter of going unwillingly; if one lives with hope, one will naturally go that way.
 The natural course of life is designed to align with the path of the will, but due to the fall, humanity began to walk an unnatural path. Here, the content of indemnity is pursued to seek re-engagement with the path of the will, which is the direction of history after the fall of humanity. Therefore, history will not become easier as it progresses; it will become increasingly difficult. The history of the individual is tragic, but the history of the family will also be tragic, and the history of the family will be tragic, leading to tragic outcomes for tribes, nations, and even the world. This is how we see it.
 So when will the end be? It will be a time of global tribulation. A time of global devastation will come. We can anticipate a time of chaos and destruction that can be said to be more difficult than any in world history based on these principles. So what time is it now? We can surmise that it is precisely that time.
 Returning to the position of Abel, when we consider Abel's position regarding the will, did Abel clearly understand God's will? That is the question. Did he understand it clearly? He did not understand it clearly. Why did God not teach him clearly? He did not clearly understand.
Did you make it from your seat? This is because it is within the principle-result subject authority that the Unification Church speaks of, and since it is God's position to probe only the results of the principle until the stages of resurrection, growth, and completion, it cannot be directly taught. Therefore, you must know it for sure. If you do not know it for sure, you must go and awaken to it, but the path of awakening is not a smooth and reasonable one. Absolutely not.

If humans in the fallen world could awaken in a glorious position under the reasonable environmental conditions they demand, how wonderful would that be? If there had been no fall, that could be possible. If one had gone through a reasonable process, one could awaken to it in a glorious position, but because of the fall, this has been reversed. Therefore, to understand the will, one must walk the path of suffering. It is through encountering all the conditions that can lament the various slanders and sorrows in the human world, digesting them while loving heaven and seeking the will, that there is a way to awaken to the will. You must understand that you cannot awaken on the path of living comfortably, receiving blessings by believing in Jesus.

Since the world was created by principle, salvation is also achieved by principle. So what is the path of religion? The more true a religion is, the more it develops through suffering. Why does it develop? Because development is in accordance with the will. It develops because God is with it. This is a fact that we can understand as the underlying content of religious history up to now. Do you understand what I mean?

You cannot awaken to the will on the path of reason; it is through the path of paradox... Everything is not decided based on theoretical standards, but after going through the paradoxical course, after undergoing indemnity and restoration, is when right and wrong are determined. You must understand that this principle started from Abel. History begins with this issue from the individual to the family, to the tribe, to the nation, or to the world, and remains until it reaches God's heart world. You must understand that there are eight stages of the process remaining.

Such a tremendous providential wall is blocking the way. Therefore, from God's perspective, God encounters humans at a position where such a wall can be overcome and passed. You must know this. In order to carry out the providence of individual salvation for us humans, God crosses over the providential walls that are layered upon each other. He comes over and meets me.

How is the spirit world currently? You must know that numerous ranks of the spirit world are being formed and covering the human world. Everything that can connect the entire spirit world to the hell on this earth is piled up in the clouds, covered by something great, what should I say, a veil. What is covering is not just one thing. There is a personal veil, a family veil, a tribal veil, then a national veil, a global veil, and when entering the spirit world, there is also a veil of the heavenly world.

In order for heaven to approach us, it must go through all these covered processes of the spirit world and through all these paths of suffering, and it is only then that it contacts my individual self, something we have never even dreamed of in our faith life. We thought, 'God is omniscient and omnipotent, so He will do as He pleases.' But what can happen just as He pleases?

Since it is a world created centered on principle, the providence of salvation is a providence of restoration, and since the providence of restoration is a history of re-creation, God cannot carry out this work apart from the principle. In order to go through all this, God Himself cannot avoid the position of fighting against Satan. Today, when we speak of a providential process, Satan accuses. In order for God to possess this, He must fulfill the conditions of indemnity, and in order to break through the global walls, heaven must fulfill the conditions of indemnity.

The history of indemnity and restoration must be achieved by naturally subjugating Cain. Who has done this work until now? It is because the archangel fell and Adam and Eve, this human world was ruined, that the angel is carrying out this work. The angelic world is carrying out this work. Therefore, the angelic world is in confrontation with Satan. The evil Satan and the good angel are in confrontation. Only after the good angels win in that battle can there be progress. Do you understand what I mean? God cannot do as He pleases. That is the principle.

Originally, humans are meant to dominate angels. They are meant to be the subject. They should also be the subject in will and in heart, but the one who fell in will is the fallen Adam and Eve, and the one who fell in heart is Adam and Eve. Therefore, in order to face the will and God, one must have the point of unity not from the fallen standard but from the point of unity of the original standard. One must have a heartistic unity at the original standard, but Satan accuses that they could not stand in such a position. This condition also applies to angels. It is not only applicable to humans but to beings related to the fallen.

Therefore, when Satan attacks, asking, 'Have you stood at the point of unity of the will?' one must be able to say, 'I have stood.' For God's will, I will go through any path of suffering. While Satan has gone centered on himself in the path of the will, I am not in the same position as you; I am going beyond myself to God,' and one must be absolute. Satan is the opposite. 'Oh, what is that absolute will? What is that? Just do it moderately like me, and whenever it is difficult in the providence of restoration, just throw it away!' Even if there are all sorts of oppositions, all of that must be removed. One must be able to go beyond it from a position that is not influenced or related to it at all. Angels can do that.

So it must come down this way, upside down. From the spirit world, through the world, through the nation... The world is all like that now. Because of the fall, in order for us to go through the will of the providence of restoration now... There is an angelic spirit world, and then there is the world, and then there is the nation, and there is the tribe, and in front of the tribe, there is the family, and in front of the family, there is the individual. Therefore, in order to find me, one must go through all these numerous stages and be connected. You must understand this, do you understand what I mean?

Today, people believe that just by believing in religion, they will be saved, but it is not that simple. If it were that simple, God would not have created this world like this until now; it would have all been resolved. Understanding the will is also realized through a paradoxical course. This is to understand the will in the midst of pain and emptiness. No matter how severe that pain is, it is impossible to fall into despair or collapse in the position of suffering. It is in the midst of pain that one understands.

For this reason, true religion goes straight through the stamp of suffering, through the valley of suffering. It is not going back and forth. If the heart goes back and forth, then the path will also go back and forth, right? Only a religion that can go straight through the valley of the process of suffering can be a true religion. Why is that? Because Abel must come through Cain. That is because the archangel, who should have been under Adam's dominion, has dominantly ruled in reverse.

In order to restore this, Abel, who is in the position of Adam, must subjugate Cain, but it must be a natural subjugation, not a forced one. The fall was forced by the archangel, but God must naturally subjugate the opposite. That is the problem. If it were possible to subjugate by force, the history would have been restored in an instant today. It must be a natural subjugation.

But who is the Cain that must be subjugated? He is the elder brother. This is a chronic pain. If he were the younger brother, one could say, 'You little brat! You must listen to your elder brother!' and even if one punches him and drags him forcibly, that would not violate the law of principle. Do you understand? From the perspective of principle, since Cain is the elder brother, the younger brother cannot just subjugate him as he pleases; such a hardship has arisen. Therefore, from a reasonable standpoint... The elder brother has all the wealth, but having fallen, he has become the property of Satan. Now, the younger brother, who is naked and has nothing, cannot come and say, 'Brother, that is mine, so give it to me!' In order for it to become the younger brother's, the elder must be naturally subjugated, but what does he have? In serving God's will, there is eternal and unchanging value, and in facing the will, one must digest any suffering. In the process of digestion, it is not for me to go to heaven. It must be for God. The content is different.

Today, when asking general religious people, 'Why do you suffer by believing?' they say, 'Oh, if I endure suffering, I will receive great blessings when I go to the afterlife.' But that is not the case. The content is fundamentally different. In suffering, I do not suffer to receive blessings; I suffer to liberate God, for God, and we must understand this clearly.

Today, people who believe in religion all think they will go to heaven by believing in Jesus and receive blessings, but it does not work that way. They must inherit the position of the elder brother. It is not about taking away. It is about inheriting. When inheriting, just as Adam would inherit with love in front of his beloved sons and daughters, just as God gives love in inheritance, if one does not inherit with love from Cain, the original standard of the will cannot be fulfilled. It cannot be established. Do you understand what I mean?

Therefore, one must have the notion that 'what I must inherit is great, but the suffering I endure is very little.' One stands in a position to inherit the vast will of God's work and God's love and the entire creation world.

So, through whom does that will come? It comes through Cain. Who is Cain? He is the one who opposes the most. He is Satan. You must know that he appears as the greatest enemy before me. Cain does not treat me with love. 'Oh, that guy! I never thought of that... He is trying to kill me in any way possible... He is trying to put me in a dead environment and just destroy me.'

As that time comes, does anyone think that the time of great will is coming? Does anyone think that God is establishing good contractual conditions that can recognize me? Is there anyone among the religious people of this world today, among Christians, or among Unification Church members? How is it? You all know well. This is the problem. Many ordinary people, those who have devoted themselves, are all breaking apart here.

Because such barriers remain, the history of humanity, the history of the providence of salvation, has not seen the fulfillment of the will throughout a long history and is rolling down into the pit of destruction. How difficult it is to put the brakes on this and stop it. It cannot be done by God alone, nor can it be done by humans alone, and even if God and humans work together, it is difficult.

Now, our Unification Church is hated by the established churches for no reason, right? But I do not speak ill of the established churches. For the past 35 years since liberation, 35 years, right? Since it is now the 1980s, it has been 35 years, and if they have opposed so much for 35 years, one would get tired of it, but why am I not tired? (Laughter) Why? Why? Just as God bestowed the great work of the creation of the universe centered on His will and with a heart of love to Adam and Eve, the Cain who becomes an enemy must say, 'Ah! My younger brother is lovely!' and 'That guy! Reverend Moon is indeed hateful, but still, when I look at it, I do not know if he believes in God or not, but he seems different from the God I believe in, yet he is quite steadfast in his public position!' They must compare and see.

'Even if my wife opposes me at home, my children oppose me, my relatives oppose me, my country opposes me, the world opposes me, that guy is going with a firm determination! He is not going back and forth. Wow—' they must be made to think. So I just want to pray for them whenever I have time, and if I have time, I want to think of them, and if they need money, I want to help them even if it means spending money. That is something that will be known later.

But what about Satan? He keeps teaching, 'Hey, your younger brother is trying to steal your property and take everything from you.' But when you look closely, there is not just Satan, is there? There is a natural heart that can return to God, so when viewed with love, one thinks, 'How can that guy be better than me?' and finally begins to think in reverse. We think one by one, but they think in reverse. 'Wow! In this aspect, I am like this, but that guy is better in that aspect. He is better in this aspect. Wow, more than half of him is better than me. If I were him, I would do this.' They keep colliding. 'Wow! He is also better!' Then they collide again and say, 'He is better in another aspect! He is better in another aspect! Oh my!' (Laughter)

To subjugate and overcome the path of suffering is the destiny of restoration. Today, to subjugate Satan, who has not been subdued for 6,000 years of biblical history, one must gather all the essence of suffering, the core of suffering, and even if one collides with it all at once, unless a person who can digest it comes forth, it is impossible to find a person who can face the will victorious over the 6,000 years of history. That is the most theoretical.

Do you understand what I mean? It is a bit difficult to understand. Just like the essence of suffering that comes from the story, even if all of this clings like a sticky substance, unless there is a person who can digest it and remain, and who can have hope instead of despair, it is from that position that the emergence of the will is possible. Does this sound absurd to you?

Therefore, Cain must be subdued. Abel must go through the traditional history that must pass through the path of suffering. That is why a person like the teacher knows this, so even if he faces worldwide opposition, even if the world opposes...

You all want the will to be realized quickly, right? 'How nice it would be if it were realized quickly! Oh, the omnipotent God will do it all! I will just sit still and watch...' But it does not work that way. If you want it to happen quickly, you must have the faith that can digest and overcome this suffering path. You must have the faith that says, 'Come on!' even if you are tortured, 'Hit me! You brat!' You must have that kind of faith. Now, we must go beyond the 35-year peak to the 40-year peak. Do you understand? If connected until three years after 1985, it will go until 1988.
This is how I see it.
Isn't it boring? Everyone, when it rains, even if it rains for just about four days, people say, 'I'm bored, I'm bored.' What if it rained for about 40 days? They would complain, 'Oh my, why is this day like this? Where did this day go... Why is this day like this! It's like this again today!' If it gets to that point, in fact, after just two weeks, they would think, 'Ah! I will welcome the rain in my lifetime.' They should think like this: 'Rain, come! Come! Come a little more!' You have to think like this. 'Ah, that's my fate,' and decide to go down the path of destiny. 'It's because my fate is tough; this is my destiny,' you should think like this.

When there is a drought and the water in the fields has all dried up, would the fish in the small puddle wish, 'Oh, I hope it doesn't rain'? 'Oh, let's think like the fish in that puddle!' Is that what we should do? Since we are in the same position as the fish in the puddle, we should say, 'Rain, please come desperately! We need a downpour! God, please send down a heavy rain! Since my back hasn't filled with water yet, let it rain like big raindrops!' This is what we should be saying.

If God were to test me with rain, I would completely pass that test. 'Not just 40 days, but even if it rains for 40 years, let it come! Let it come! Even if it takes 400 years, it must come after I die and after several generations! That's how I think!' Even if it rains, I would not say to stop... Why would God conduct a test that would cause Him loss? (Laughter) God does not conduct tests that result in loss. God is a wise being. And so is Satan. If the situation is already wrong, it is wrong. No matter how hard you try, if the author is wrong, they would say, 'Ah, just forget it,' and kick it away with the left foot instead of the right foot. Do you understand what I mean?

Today, the title is 'Reflection on the History of Providence,' so when I reflect on the history of the family of Cain and Abel, I wonder how many people have realized for the first time after hearing the teacher's words that there are such puddles of stories. Raise your hands if you have realized this. Did you all already know? (Laughter) Did you know everything? 「Yes」 Oh! Thank you. Oh! That's wonderful.

When I see you saying, 'Let's have children and be blessed and live well! Let's find someone we love and live well!'... Can you really live well? Can you live well? Who guarantees that you can live well? Without confidence...

Because there are countless whirlpools of suffering in the destiny of restoration that humanity must go through, the world is not a place where you can be blessed and live as you please. The more you go, the more you collide. The collisions are not enemies. Those collisions are meant to drive you into the path of restoration through the whip of love, and when you realize this, how beneficial it will be for your life and journey. No matter how anyone stands in a position of despair and stagnation regarding God's will, they will be able to say, 'I will go.'

Despite the fact that humanity has fallen, it is amazing that there is a path of hope. Do you understand? Do you think so? That is not what traditional churches teach. It is taught by the notorious Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. In fact, it is notorious. It is not notorious before God, but notorious before Satan. Then what is it before God? Instead of notoriety, what is it? It is high reputation... That's my name! (Laughter) In that sense, Reverend Moon has a high reputation. (Laughter) It feels good, doesn't it? (Applause)

Now, you need to understand this principle, because it is a reflection. This applies to the individual standard. You cannot escape this. That is why there is a Korean proverb that says, 'When a cousin buys a field, it hurts in the stomach,' but even if they buy a plot of land instead of a rice field, it still hurts in the stomach.

Then, that saying reflects the characteristics of the Korean people. Why is that? Because the Korean people stand in the closest historical position of Cain and Abel. They engage in fratricidal conflict, and if someone is talented, they are quick to cut off their neck. They kill each other, causing a lot of bloodshed.

From this principle, isn't it the Korean nation that stands in the closest position where God and Satan can collide in the history of the providence of restoration? When you think that way, doesn't it feel good? Whether my teacher's words are right or wrong, it feels good because it sounds plausible. If it is true, how good would that be? The Value and Importance of Home Church 
Are you all doing home church? Raise your hands if you are doing home church activities. Raise your hands if you are engaged in home church activities. Have you all received local placements? "Yes." Today, I’d like to talk a bit about home church. 
Why do we need home church? 
The home church that our Unification Church has will be a content that no religion, denomination, or religious organization can possess. So why do we need home church? That’s the question. Why is home church necessary? 
Originally, the providence of salvation arose because of the fall of humanity, so the providence of salvation was established due to the fall. What is salvation? It is the restoration to the original state. However, restoration does not just happen; it occurs through the principle of re-creation, that is, through the process of the principle of re-creation. This is what I see as the essence of the providence of salvation. 
Then what is the principle of re-creation? What is re-creation? It is necessary to recreate because we have deviated from the principles of creation. To recreate, what position must we stand in? We must stand in God’s position to recreate. This conclusion arises. However, since we are in a fallen position, we cannot stand in the position to re-create. In other words, re-creation can only happen from a position that represents God. 
Then how can fallen humanity represent God’s position? Ultimately, it is through a step-by-step position, that is, through individual, family, and tribal stages, that the providential environment expands along with historical development. What is the position that can represent God in our Unification Church? That is the position of Abel. In contrast, what is the position that can represent Satan? That is the position of Cain. 
So what is the fall? It is humanity’s submission to Satan. More than just submission to Satan, it is a change of position. Therefore, what is the providence of salvation? It is to turn back to God’s position. 
Who turns back? It is not God Himself who turns back, but it is humanity who fell that turns back. Therefore, I believe that without the unity of humanity and God, the providence of salvation cannot be fulfilled. The position of Abel is the position representing God, so through Abel, the history of subjugating Cain in a relative position unfolds. If Cain is not subdued, Abel has no ownership. 
Originally, if Adam had not fallen, he would have been the center of the universe and could have owned even God. God should be the God of Adam. Therefore, Adam could have stood in a privileged position to own God’s love, but due to the fall, he lost everything. Because Adam could not own, all the achievements created by God should have belonged to God, but they could not belong to God and instead became Satan’s along with fallen humanity. Therefore, here we must carry out the movement to restore ownership. 
The movement to restore ownership over the world, ownership over humanity, and ownership over God—this is what I see as the providence of salvation. If humanity had not fallen, originally, God would belong to humanity, humanity would belong to God, all things would belong to humanity, and also to God. All of this comes from one. 
If God and humanity had become one, everything would belong to God and to me, but because it was lost due to the fall, it must be restored again. I see it this way. Based on this background, God has been carrying out providential history in the human world, so the history of the human world cannot help but have a corresponding background. 
The history so far has been a history of war centered on ownership. 
So what have fallen humans held in the history of humanity so far? The issue of ownership, the issue of ownership over material. What has been the central target of the wars that humans have fought until now, woven into the history of war? It has been material. This is how it has been. Isn’t that so? "I want to be a great nation, I want to be a great nation" ultimately means what? It means to become a people standing on a foundation of having a lot of land centered on national foundations. Everyone is saying that. 
So what has been the problem so far? It is that we have been carrying out a history of struggle centered on material. However, until now, humans have not realized this. No one has known that through some actions behind history, certain phenomena and processes have unfolded in the course of history. They thought it was just because humans were born from each other. 
Then why is history a history of war? The fact that history has been woven into a history of war can lead to a position that denies God. That problem is very complex. Until now, history has been a history of struggle for establishing ownership, and to turn the ownership of evil, the ownership of the world of evil, into the ownership of the world of good, we must turn back the history of the struggle between good and evil. 
Then how is the method of struggle between good and evil different? Evil fights centered on itself for its own benefit, while good is about the relative rights,
This may be a bit difficult to understand, but it is about fighting not for oneself but for the greater good of others. 
Why is that? When we look at this issue, it connects to various complex problems such as the dual purpose mentioned in our principle of creation. Leaving that aside... Ultimately, good and evil are in conflict, with evil trying to maintain its position from the standpoint of pursuing its own interests, while the good side is trying to transform this into ownership for the whole. That is why there is a struggle. God is centered on the whole, while evil is centered on the individual.

At the point of good and evil, the value of evil can be said to lie in its self-centeredness and its ability to draw others in. So what about good? The foundation of good is formed by trying to apply value to the other side. They are in complete opposition. A person who lives for themselves belongs to evil, while a person who lives for the whole belongs to good.

So why should it be this way? It would be nice if heaven stood in a position that favors itself, but why should heaven stand in a position that favors the whole? This is the ideal of creation. What does the realization of ideals mean? There is no ideal that focuses solely on the perfection of my individual self. The realization of ideals occurs in the perfection of the other.

Isn't that right? Students who study say, "I study hard to become a great person," but just because they become a PhD doesn't mean they are a great person. Even if they become a PhD, when they take on the subjectivity of the greater good, when they stand in a subjective position, only then can they realize the ideals they have studied. Therefore, the efforts being made now are for relative purposes. Isn't that so? A farmer who sows seeds is ultimately sowing towards the relative purpose of being able to harvest in the fall. This is the focal point of the cosmic phenomenon or the world of action.

That is why a good person is someone who is not self-centered. If one becomes a good companion, it is not about saying, "Hey, do whatever you want. Do this your way, do that your way!" Telling someone to do as they please does not make them a good companion or a good person. The standard of good is formed when one sacrifices oneself and acts for others, for friends. Everything happens based on this principle. And when we say "a good citizen," what kind of citizen is a good citizen? It is not one who only cares for themselves, but one who has a foundation to cooperate with the entire nation.

So what happens when one is good? Goodness expands. It must expand. Fortune circulates. Because it is round, goodness must expand. What happens when it expands? It comes back. When it comes back, what happens? It does not go around without me; when it goes around, it pushes me forward. It is a circulating fortune, and it does not just disappear at the end but comes back and pushes me forward. From that perspective, it ultimately becomes something that benefits me. I am formed in a position that can represent the whole.

Then did God create an environment that can represent the whole? That is the universe. When God created the universe, what did He create? He created an environment. Within the environment... what did He do by creating the environment? He established subjects and objects. It is simple. This universe is for establishing subjects and objects.

So why does the environment of the Republic of Korea exist? It is to establish subjects and objects centered on humanity. That is a sovereign state. It becomes a social organization. Everything is a combination of subjective people and relative rights forming an organizational form, which is the existence and way of existence of the universe. If it is a world, the same principle applies. In a global environment, there must be some kind of subjective existence and relative rights formed to create the world. Therefore, the issue of the rights or ideals of a subject that can lead the world arises.

When we look at all humanity, we see it is dualistic. It is made up of mind and body. The expansion of this mind and body, according to our principle, is called a microcosm, and when the inner aspect of this microcosm expands, it encompasses the spirit world and the entire universe. In this environment, when we view humanity and the whole through the principle of subject and object, if God exists, God would be the subject, and humanity would be in the position of the object. And God and humanity must become one.

So what will happen when they become one? Becoming one is not temporary but eternal. It is about pursuing an eternity that transcends time. It must be this way. What should the subjective content that pursues that eternity be? When we look at this issue, it is knowledge, but it is not knowledge. It is said to be knowledge, money, power, but it is not these. It must be love. What parents need in a family is not their faces, not the face of the father, not the physical body of the parents, but the love that emanates from those parents. Isn't that right?

When a man needs a wife, does he need a wife who is loving, a wife who is likable, or a wife who is studious, or a wife who is good with money? There may be various types, but it is not a likable or studious wife. It is a loving wife. In that loving wife, everything is encompassed. When we talk about the ideal family, what does that mean? Separation of Good and Evil

Today, I would like to speak briefly on the topic of "Separation of Good and Evil." Can you hear me? "I can't hear you." You can't hear me? My voice is a bit hoarse because I spoke a lot yesterday. Fallen humanity must go through the providential course of salvation
We know that religion arose due to the fall, and that the providence of salvation naturally emerged from it. The providence of salvation is a movement to return to the original state centered on the Messiah, and we understand that the Messiah has continued the central history of the providence of salvation. Fallen humanity, regardless of who it is, must go through the course of providence for salvation, and to do so, it must be united with the Messiah.

The Messiah is ultimately a central figure to establish a relationship between heaven and myself. Here, we come to feel the existence of heaven, the Messiah, and myself. My existence is connected to the world of Satan through this central figure of heaven and the Messiah. When I look at myself from this perspective, what I need is the Messiah and God. What I do not need is the negative self, the self that opposes good, and Satan. We must understand that we are in this position. You must recognize that my current position is one that connects two worlds.

Therefore, everyone follows a path of learning or education, and what is the purpose of that? It is to advance toward a better world. It is to possess more valuable content. Thus, the determination to advance to a higher dimension is to align with a more valuable center. We know that we are on a path of pursuing such goals, even if indirectly.

Furthermore, to believe in religion means to believe in order to pursue more internal values. Therefore, we understand that religion is a commitment to the path of pursuing internal values. Then, who is the ultimate being of this internal pursuit? It is neither the Messiah nor God. This is how it is. When viewed in relation to the external world, I stand in the position of the Messiah and myself. Therefore, we must become one with the internal God and the external representative of God, the Messiah.

So, who should be the center around which we become one? We cannot become one centered on fallen humanity. We must become one centered on the Messiah and God. The Messiah becomes one with God, and centered on that Messiah, I become one with the Messiah, thereby connecting my inner self to the external God through the external Messiah. The self is the turning point of good and evil
Then, why is it that we cannot become one with God directly? It is because we have fallen. This is the problem. We want to become one with God directly, but fallen humanity requires a mediator. So, what is the content needed as a mediator? It is necessary for the pursuit of new life and new love. The love you pursue centered on the life you were born into is self-centered love. It stops at self-centered love. Where does self-centered love lead? It does not go toward heaven; it flows toward Satan.

We must understand that this is the human condition belonging to a fallen lineage and fallen realm. Therefore, the self is a turning point between two worlds. It is the turning point of two worlds. What I say is inevitably divided into two. What I see is also divided into two, and what I hear is all divided into two. My thoughts do not always center around the direction of good; they fluctuate back and forth. I think this way at times and that way at other times. Sometimes I think of what my body desires, and at other times I think of what my heart desires. This is how we are in conflict.

So, how does a true human think? A true human thinks from a position where the heart and body are united. The direction of thought when the heart and body are united is clear throughout the day and in every aspect of life. Whether in childhood, youth, adulthood, or old age, the direction should be consistent throughout one’s life, which was the original human state before the fall. However, the human condition today after the fall is zigzagging every day. It is fluctuating back and forth.

If you observe yourself, you will see that you also think in two ways. You think of your family in two ways, and you think of the society you live in that way as well. Today, the Republic of Korea itself is following that path. It does not know where to go; it is fluctuating. Today, the world is also going that way. Therefore, I must be good. This is the problem.

Today, humanity has become full of contradictions because we have fallen.

The Reason Korea is Blessed  
One more thing I want to say is why Korea is blessed. Look, how did Rome, which dominated the ancient world, remain a powerful nation until now? If we look at the climate of Rome, it has distinct spring, summer, autumn, and winter. It has a climate similar to Korea. The spring season is clear, the summer season is clear, the autumn season is clear, and the winter season is clear.  
Geographically, considering the climate, the best region is this peninsula called Italy. Why is that? Such a region can serve as a foundation for producing comprehensive cultural achievements. What does that mean? It can absorb and integrate tropical, temperate, and polar civilizations.  
This cultural development circles the world. Historically, I cannot explain everything due to time constraints. It goes around the world. From one starting point to the conclusion, the result and the cause must align.  
In this regard, Italy, due to its favorable climatic conditions, has contributed to the culture of the world. Similarly, if we look at Korea, which is located in the eastern hemisphere, it has a climatic background that is relatively similar to Italy. It is fascinating. Korea has spring, summer, autumn, and winter, and during the winter season, there is a formal climate called "three cold and three warm" that moves the winter season. This is an astonishing fact.  
Therefore, considering these climatic conditions, Korea has the potential to become the vanguard of a new era that can inherit the newly circulating morning civilization, that is, spring civilization! I see it this way. (Applause)  
Now, let’s look at Korea. It is directly confronting communism. This is not Italy. Why is the Korean Peninsula facing such problems? It is suffering under the harsh cold winds of polar civilization, but if it can possess the seed of life and break through, a new era of spring civilization that has never existed in human history will come. I refer to this as the "Cultural Era of the Middle Kingdom." I believe that a cultural era that can harmonize everything will come.  
If civilization progresses according to climate, and if that is true, then from this climatic perspective, Korea can become a base for creating a new culture.  
In this view, the Korean Peninsula is in a duel of life and death with communism. Am I to disappear before your gun, or will I absorb your gun and sprout with life? I see it as being in such a position.  
Then, a powerful country like the United States cannot ignore Korea. The country that occupies Korea in the Far East will dominate Asia. That is why Japan also values Korea. Isn’t that right? And China also values it.
The Soviet Union also valued it. The Russo-Japanese War and the Sino-Japanese War all happened because of Korea, didn’t they? This is quite an unusual content. After liberation, various regimes passed through, but it was centered around the Park regime that raised the banner of global revival. It wasn’t just because President Park was capable; it was because the time of fortune had come. The time of fortune has arrived. The fact that we were able to revive the nation in a short period was due to a natural, fortuitous background that our people may not be aware of, but which supported Park. That’s how I see it.

Centered around the victory ideology, the three generations must be connected. So, what is the Unification Church today? What is the Victory Federation today? We have the potential to digest the democratic world, digest communism, and become the vanguard of creating a new civilization with subjectivity! If there is a stronger organization than the Unification Church, I don’t know, but in the Republic of Korea, there is nothing stronger than this…. This is global. This should not be limited to the nation. At the same time, considering the global background and the cultural historical background, if we present a new systematic ideology that surpasses the theories of communism and the Christian thoughts of the democratic world, on the day we can digest communism and the democratic world, Korea will remain as a leading base for cultural creation in the new era, in this Pacific era, just as the Italian peninsula was the base for cultural creation that dominated the world! That’s how I see it. (Applause)

Now, let’s return to yourselves. Can you digest communism? Can you digest the Christian cultural sphere? You need to know this. You cannot be ignorant of this; you must know. You need to understand the deep essence of communism. The democratic world is a Christian cultural sphere—understanding the deep essence here and possessing the subjectivity to digest it will unite the world.

Interestingly, Buddhism has come to Korea and has borne fruit, Confucianism has come and borne fruit, and Christianity has come and borne fruit. All of them have moved the nation. Recently, Islam has also come in. They are all clashing with each other. Islam is exotic. But what can they unite under? They cannot unite under political power. The only way to unite is under the title of anti-communism, victory ideology. In this world era, all religions must come together and make a joint resolution. (Applause) Do you understand?

When the Korean people, who can be the main actors, possess subjectivity, the problem becomes significant. That’s why I have been hoping for such a time and have fought until now. I hope that all of you, the prominent figures across the nation, feel that the fact that you have gathered here today and made a new resolution is the beginning of a higher dimension of a new historical era.

Therefore, you must connect the three generations. In living, there is a past, a present, and a future. There must be a father above and a child below. You must maintain good contact among these three generations. In this regard, while you are important, the question is how you will raise your sons and daughters.

Even if you have decided on a direction to serve the country here today, your children have not yet made that decision. What I earnestly hope for is to bring just 3,000 talented individuals with brilliant minds from the Republic of Korea and educate them. I believe that if we educate them for about six months, we can cultivate leading figures who can move the world.

Now, looking at the current foundation of our Unification Church, I started as a subject as an Asian Korean, but if Korean youth had become the wings and the foundation, if they had appeared before many countries of the world armed with ideology, Korea would already have stood in the position of a subject that can lead the entire world.

However, this did not happen, so I have put forward Japanese and German people. I have placed Japanese and Germans at the forefront over Americans. Americans are too scattered. They are indifferent. There is no order. Japanese people inherit the actions of warriors and have a hierarchy. When orders come from above, there is no objection.

Also, when a purpose is presented to the Germanic people, they have ambitions to aggregate and elevate it to a global level. In terms of nationalism, warriors face it boldly. Look. The Germanic people cannot be subdued by any ethnicity. Whether it’s England, France, or Italy, they all look down from above and possess the ability to rise to the highest position in the world.

What I find most disappointing is that if the Republic of Korea had supported me until now, even just three years ago, we would have laid this entire foundation. Now, it is not too late, so if there are excellent individuals among your children, we must train them in victory ideology and arm them with thought to welcome the new era of Chinese civilization, the springtime civilization era. If we recognize that the foundation for a cultural era that God and humanity desire has been vaguely laid based on Korean soil, we must gather our children.

This is not to serve the Unification Church. Until now, I have never taught that I should live for the Unification Church or act for the Unification Church. Religion must exist for the nation. Religion must save the nation, the nation must save the world, and the world must save heaven. We must save heaven. This is how I see it.

Therefore, members of the Unification Church have a clear understanding of this. Whether day or night, they are striving to walk this path. Because of this, as this movement connects across the world beyond the nation, even though the distance is far, it will gradually narrow, and when we can stand in a place where we can speak to each other from east to west, think about what will happen to this world. The fact that you have traveled like this for a day or two is an amazing fact.

Similarly, what I do in America is the same. All parents say that Reverend Moon brainwashes their children. They say he brainwashes them. What kind of brainwashing is that? It is because it has a higher-level theory. You must understand that. The ideology of the Unification Church is vast, more so than those who have graduated from any university or hold any doctoral degree. It is vast. It is vast.

The free democratic world, the ins and outs of history, or the ins and outs of the philosophical world, all of these can be systematized from a dreamlike world into the reality stage, where one can sense the existence of God through the feelings of life. Do you understand what that means? Therefore, God is our Father. The era of an abstract God has passed. We must discover an empirical, life-leading God. That God is the subject, and those who possess the value of the object and have the ability to digest anything, if they are born among your descendants on this peninsula, it is evident that they will dominate the world. This is an undeniable fact.

You must have the pride of being the vanguard of the era of Chinese civilization. Knowing this, if you, the central figures, return to your regions and connect one or two people—especially if you have sons and daughters, that would be even better—and position them to be sent to the world as the vanguard of the new era, how wonderful would that be? Do you understand? “Yes.” (Applause)

Please have that perspective; Korea must have the confidence to be a hopeful nation in the future. Korea is the nation that will be the vanguard in the new springtime civilization, the era of Chinese civilization. If we become suitable elders and educate our children, instilling ideology so that we can become a nation that can digest the world within Korea, this nation will lead all countries in history and be revered by all nations.

By doing so, it will be possible to form the nation that God loves the most, this is how I see it. This is the perspective I desire. Do you understand? You are all Koreans, so you will wish for that. If that does not happen, I will create it. I will make it. We can make it with our strength.

Knowing this, please return and support the young people…. When we look at our young people, they may not seem impressive in your eyes. Of course, they lack social experience. They lack social experience. They are not equipped in every aspect. However, we must respect the thoughts they possess. We must respect the thoughts they have…. Regardless of what anyone says, they possess the vitality to pursue this path to the end, something that communism cannot digest and that no one in the democratic world can digest. We must respect the fact that they have even a vague sense of that and nurture them even more, even if they do not reach your level. Someone must help them. There must be a teacher. Someone must nurture them.

One of the undesirable traits of Korean people is that they tend to eliminate those who are better than themselves. They try to eliminate those who are better than them. That cannot happen. We must play the game of nurturing them. Now, if you resolve today and return, saying many people will do this, new springs will emerge in each province, don’t you think? This is how I see it.

I would be grateful if you could focus your hearts on such matters and make efforts. Thank you. (Applause) *
